## 第93题 (ID: 244901)

### 中文题目

“第一期货有限公司”是期交所参与者。判断以下哪些情形属于其应遵守的“一般责任”？
I. 根据期交所董事会指示，向期交所提供其与海外某交易所资料共享协议所要求的客户资料。
II. 当其公司注册地址变更时，立即通知期交所。
III. 按证监会要求，提交最近一年的全部交易电话录音。
IV. 按期交所行政总裁要求，提交根据《操守准则》规定须备存的账簿。
A. I,II,III
B. I,II,IV
C. I,III,IV
D. II,III,IV


### English

"First Futures Limited" is an HKFE participant. Which of the following situations fall under its "general obligations"?
I. Provide client information required under a data-sharing agreement with an overseas exchange to the HKFE as directed by the HKFE Board.
II. Immediately notify the HKFE when its company registered address changes.
III. Submit all trade-related telephone recordings for the past year as required by the SFC.
IV. Submit books required under the Code of Conduct as requested by the Chief Executive of the HKFE.
A. I,II,III
B. I,II,IV
C. I,III,IV
D. II,III,IV


**正确答案：B**


### 答案解析

I 正确。根据《期交所规则》，参与者须按董事会指示向期交所提供资料共享安排所要求的资料。
II 正确。申请表格中的资料如有变动，须即时通知期交所。
III 错误。提交电话录音是《操守准则》要求，但题干未提及是期交所行政总裁或指定员工的要求。该责任是按要求提交，而非自动按证监会要求提交。
IV 正确。按期交所行政总裁或指定员工要求，提交包括《操守准则》规定的簿册及文件。


### Explanation

I is correct. Under HKFE rules, participants must provide information required under data-sharing arrangements to the HKFE as directed by the Board.
II is correct. Any change in information provided in the application form must be immediately notified to the HKFE.
III is incorrect. Submitting telephone recordings is a Code of Conduct requirement, but the scenario does not specify it is requested by the HKFE Chief Executive or designated staff. The obligation is to submit upon request, not automatically to the SFC.
IV is correct. Submit books and documents, including those required under the Code of Conduct, as requested by the HKFE Chief Executive or designated staff.


### 温习册出处

期交所参与者的持续责任
《期交所规则》列载期交所参与者应遵守的“一般责任”。
各期交所参与者须遵守以下的一般责任：
(h) 于期交所董事会的指示下，向期交所提供与香港交易及结算所有限公司（“香港交易所”）或期交所已签订资料共用安排或协议的交易所、监管机构或组织（不论是否在香港）要求的任何资料；
(i) 倘期交所作出要求，须在其载于期交所参与者资格申请表格中提供（不论是申请期交所参与者资格时提供或任何其后时间提供）的资料出现任何变动时，即时通知期交所；及
(j) 呈交有关报表及／或期交所行政总裁或任何其他指定香港交易所员工所要求的簿册、纪录、账目及文件，包括根据《证券及期货事务监察委员会持牌人或注册人操守准则》（“《操守准则》”）规定须予备存的簿册、账目及电话纪录。


---

## 第94题 (ID: 244902)

### 中文题目

某期交所参与者的公司董事李先生，因个人投资失败，已被法院裁定破产。该公司管理层刚刚获悉此事。根据期交所参与者须遵守的一般责任，该公司应如何应对？
A. 立即召开董事会讨论李先生的继任人选，并在确定人选后内部通告。
B. 由于李先生个人破产不影响公司运营，公司无需采取任何特别行动。
C. 即时以书面形式通知期交所其董事破产事宜。
D. 只需在年度合规报告中提及此事即可。


### English

A director of a Futures Exchange participant company, Mr. Li, has been adjudicated bankrupt by the court due to personal investment failures. The company&#039;s management has just learned of this matter. According to the general responsibilities that a Futures Exchange participant must comply with, how should the company respond?
A. Convene a board meeting immediately to discuss Mr. Li&#039;s successor and issue an internal announcement once the successor is determined.
B. Since Mr. Li&#039;s personal bankruptcy does not affect the company&#039;s operations,the company need not take any special action.
C. Immediately notify the Futures Exchange in writing of the bankruptcy of its director.
D. It is sufficient to mention this matter in the annual compliance report.


**正确答案：C**


### 答案解析

A错误。虽然需要处理董事变更，但规则明确要求将此事件本身即时书面通知期交所，这是首要的直接责任。
B错误。董事破产是需要即时书面通知期交所的指定事件之一，不能以不影响运营为由不报告。
C正确。根据一般责任，当期交所参与者知悉其任何董事破产时，须即时以书面形式通知期交所。
D错误。年度报告周期太长，不符合“即时”通知的要求。


### Explanation

A is incorrect. While handling the director&#039;s succession is needed, the rules explicitly require immediate written notification to the Futures Exchange of the event itself as a primary direct responsibility.
B is incorrect. The bankruptcy of a director is one of the specified events requiring immediate written notification to the Futures Exchange. It cannot be unreported on the grounds of not affecting operations.
C is correct. According to the general responsibilities, when a Futures Exchange participant becomes aware of the bankruptcy of any of its directors, it must immediately notify the Futures Exchange in writing.
D is incorrect. The annual reporting cycle is too long and does not meet the requirement for "immediate" notification.


### 温习册出处

期交所参与者的持续责任
《期交所规则》列载期交所参与者应遵守的“一般责任”。
各期交所参与者须遵守以下的一般责任：
(g) 在发生以下任何一项或多项事宜时，即时以书面形式通知期交所：
(i) 知悉违反任何期交所规则、《证券及期货条例》及其附属法例，以及期交所施加的条件；
(ii) 通过任何决议案、展开任何法律诉讼而可能令致期交所参与者或其任何股东的财产接收人（或等同者）获委任，或导致期交所参与者或其任何股东遭清盘（或等同事件），或获颁任任何接管令或与债权人达成任何债务偿还安排或债务重整协议；
(iii) 其任何董事破产；
(iv) 其知悉任何其他期交所参与者任何违反《期交所规则》或《证券及期货条例》及其附属法例；
(v) 其知悉任何根据《期交所规则》须通知期交所、其董事会或其行政总裁的事宜；
(vi) 发生任何根据《证券及期货条例》及／或《财政资源规则》须通知证监会的事件；
(vii) 任何监管机构或其他专业或行业团体对其施加任何纪律处分措施，或拒绝、暂停或撤回其业务所需之任何监管牌照、许可或批准；
(viii)期交所董事会可能不时指定的任何其他事件；及
(ix) 其 HKATS 电子交易系统设备或任何其他设备、系统或设施的操作或运作出现任何故障或明显的故障，而这些设备、系统或设施对其业务运作极为关键；


---

## 第95题 (ID: 244903)

### 中文题目

某家期交所参与者（一家香港注册的有限公司）在运营过程中发现，由于内部系统故障，其在过去一周的某些交易可能未能完全符合HKATS电子交易系统的使用规定。根据期交所参与者应遵守的一般责任，该公司首先应该采取以下哪项行动？
A. 立即停止所有交易活动，直到系统完全修复。
B. 对相关责任人进行内部处分，并将处分结果记录在案。
C. 即时书面通知期交所其未能遵守相关规定的发现。
D. 仅需内部修复系统，确保未来合规，无需对外报告。


### English

A Futures Exchange participant (a Hong Kong registered limited company) discovers during operations that, due to an internal system failure, some of its trades in the past week may not have fully complied with the HKATS electronic trading system usage requirements. According to the general responsibilities that a Futures Exchange participant must comply with, which of the following actions should the company take first?
A. Immediately halt all trading activities until the system is fully repaired.
B. Take internal disciplinary action against the responsible personnel and document the results.
C. Immediately notify the Futures Exchange in writing of its discovery of the non-compliance.
D. Only need to repair the system internally to ensure future compliance,without external reporting.


**正确答案：C**


### 答案解析

A错误。立即停止所有交易可能是一种谨慎的应对，但规则中并未将其规定为发现不合规时的首要强制性行动。
B错误。内部处理是公司管理行为，但规则强调的是向交易所报告的责任。
C正确。根据一般责任，期交所参与者发现任何未能遵守《期交所规则》等情况时，有责任即时书面通知期交所。
D错误。规则要求将未能遵守的情况即时书面通知期交所，仅内部处理不符合此责任。


### Explanation

A is incorrect. Immediately halting all trading may be a prudent response, but it is not stipulated as the primary mandatory action upon discovering non-compliance in the rules.
B is incorrect. Internal handling is a company management action, but the rules emphasize the responsibility to report to the Exchange.
C is correct. According to the general responsibilities, a Futures Exchange participant has a duty to immediately notify the Futures Exchange in writing upon discovering any failure to comply with the Futures Exchange Rules, etc.
D is incorrect. The rules require immediate written notification to the Futures Exchange upon discovering non-compliance. Handling it internally only does not fulfill this responsibility.


### 温习册出处

期交所参与者的持续责任
《期交所规则》列载期交所参与者应遵守的“一般责任”。
各期交所参与者须遵守以下的一般责任：
(a) 严格遵守《证券及期货条例》的条文、《期交所规则》、以及其期交所参与
者资格的批准通知书中指定的任何条件，并遵守期交所董事会、期交所行政总裁及任何其他合资格人士根据《期交所规则》行使其职能时作出的决定、指示等，并且于发现任何未能遵守的情况时即时书面通知期交所；
(b) 持有至少一个期交所交易权；
(c) 为香港注册成立的有限公司，并根据《商业登记条例》持有商业登记证；
(d) 遵守《期交所规则》的规定：每名有意透过期货结算所结算本身交易的期交所参与者必须成为期货结算所的参与者，而每名非结算所参与者必须与期货结算所的相关全面结算参与者签订独立协议，后者将代表非结算所参与者结算其合约；
(e) 遵守《财政资源规则》及由期交所不时订明的其他财务要求；
(f) 遵守 HKATS 电子交易系统的所有保养、运作、使用及保障规定；


---

## 第96题 (ID: 244904)

### 中文题目

某期货结算所参与者的综合客户户口中记录了大量客户持仓。根据期货结算所的标准处理流程，以下关于这些持仓状态的描述，哪一项是正确的？
A. 这些持仓将被自动进行净额结算，结算所参与者无需采取任何行动。
B. 除非该参与者另有指令，否则期货结算所会将这些持仓全部视为“未平仓”持仓。
C. 这些持仓将每天自动与参与者公司户口内的反向持仓进行对冲平仓。
D. 这些持仓的状态将由结算所根据市场波动率自动调整。


### English

A Clearing Participant&#039;s Omnibus Client Account records a large volume of client positions. According to the Clearing House&#039;s standard processing procedures, which of the following descriptions regarding the status of these positions is correct?
A. These positions will be automatically netted settled,and the Clearing Participant needs to take no action.
B. Unless the participant instructs otherwise,the Clearing House will treat all these positions as "open" positions.
C. These positions will be automatically hedged and closed out daily against opposite positions in the participant&#039;s House Account.
D. The status of these positions will be automatically adjusted by the Clearing House based on market volatility.


**正确答案：B**


### 答案解析

A错误。综合客户户口的持仓按长仓及短仓毛额基准列帐，不会自动进行净额结算。
B正确。除非期货结算所参与者向期货结算所另有指令，否则期货结算所会将该参与者的综合客户户口的所有持仓作“未平仓”持仓处理。
C错误。规则中未描述综合客户户口持仓会与公司户口持仓自动对冲。
D错误。持仓状态由参与者指令或标准规则决定，非由市场波动率自动调整。


### Explanation

A is incorrect. Positions in the Omnibus Client Account are recorded on a gross long and short basis and are not automatically net settled.
B is correct. Unless the Clearing Participant instructs the Clearing House otherwise, the Clearing House will treat all positions in the participant&#039;s Omnibus Client Account as "open" positions.
C is incorrect. The rules do not describe that positions in the Omnibus Client Account are automatically hedged against positions in the House Account.
D is incorrect. The status of positions is determined by participant instructions or standard rules, not automatically adjusted by market volatility.


### 温习册出处

各期货结算所参与者须使用综合客户户口作为其交易的专设户口。综合客户户口的持仓按长仓及短仓毛额基准列帐。除非期货结算所参与者向期货结算所另有指令，否则期货结算所会将该期货结算所参与者的综合客户户口的所有持仓作“未平仓”持仓处理。倘期货结算所参与者拟透过衍生产品结算及交收系统在综合客户户口内平仓，则须向期货结算所提交持仓调整要求。公司户口、个别客户户口及庄家户口的持仓会自动进行净额结算。期货结算所参与者无须指示期货结算所在该等户口内平仓。
此外，期货结算所亦容许下列产品之间平仓：(i)恒生指数（“恒指”）期货及小型恒指期货合约；(ii)恒指期权及小型恒指期权合约；(iii)恒生中国企业指数期货及小型恒生中国企业指数期货；及(iv)恒生中国企业指数期权及小型恒生中国企业指数期权合约。就此而言，该等产品的持仓是按 1 张恒指期货合约兑 5 张小型恒指期货合约、1 张恒指期权合约兑 5 张小型恒指期权合约、1 张恒生中国企业指数期货合约兑 5 张小型恒生中国企业指数期货合约以及 1 张恒生中国企业指数期权合约兑 5 张小型恒生中国企业指数期权合约的比例平仓。


---

## 第97题 (ID: 244905)

### 中文题目

某期货结算所参与者为多家机构客户提供结算服务。为提升运营效率并降低整体资金占用，该参与者考虑将不同客户的持仓在结算所层面进行一定程度的合并管理，同时仍需满足监管对客户资产隔离和保护的要求。根据期货结算所户口类别，该参与者可以考虑为这些客户使用以下哪种户口？
A. 公司户口
B. 综合客户户口
C. 个别客户户口
D. 庄家户口


### English

A Clearing Participant provides clearing services for several institutional clients. To improve operational efficiency and reduce overall capital usage, the participant is considering managing the positions of different clients on a somewhat consolidated basis at the clearing house level, while still needing to meet regulatory requirements for client asset segregation and protection. According to the Clearing House account categories, which type of account could the participant consider using for these clients?
A. House Account
B. Omnibus Client Account
C. Individual Client Account
D. Market Maker Account


**正确答案：B**


### 答案解析

A错误。公司户口用于记录参与者自身的公司交易及持仓，不能用于记录客户交易。
B正确。综合客户户口用于按综合基准记录期货结算所参与者客户的交易及持仓。它将不同客户的持仓在户口层面合并记录（按毛额基准收取按金），可以在一定程度上提升运营效率。
C错误。个别客户户口是按个别客户基准记录交易及持仓，每个户口仅属于一名客户，无法实现不同客户持仓的合并管理。
D错误。庄家户口用于记录参与者自身的庄家活动产生的交易及持仓，不适用于记录普通客户交易。


### Explanation

A is incorrect. The House Account is used to record the participant&#039;s own proprietary trades and positions and cannot be used to record client trades.
B is correct. The Omnibus Client Account is used to record the trades and positions of the Clearing Participant&#039;s clients on an omnibus basis. It consolidates the positions of different clients at the account level (with margins collected on a gross basis), which can improve operational efficiency to some extent.
C is incorrect. The Individual Client Account records trades and positions on an individual client basis. Each account belongs to only one client, so it cannot achieve consolidated management of different clients&#039; positions.
D is incorrect. The Market Maker Account is used to record trades and positions arising from the participant&#039;s own market-making activities and is not suitable for recording ordinary client trades.


### 温习册出处

在期货结算所的户口
期货结算所参与者在期货结算所开立户口，以进行交易登记及结算。有关户口可能属于下列不同类别的户口：
(a) 公司户口－用作记录期货结算所参与者的公司交易及持仓，并按持仓净额基准计算按金；
(b) 综合客户户口－用作按综合基准记录期货结算所参与者客户的交易及持仓，并按毛额基准收取其持仓的按金；
(c) 个别客户户口－用作按个别客户基准记录期货结算所参与者客户的交易及持仓，并按净额基准收取持仓的按金；期货结算所参与者必要确保在个别客户户口内所列帐的一切交易及持仓，仅属于一名客户，且有关交易及持仓不得由操作综合户口的客户持有；
(d) 客户按金对销户口－用作记录期货结算所参与者的个别客户属可对销性质的持仓。每个按金对销组合中的持仓必须属于同一名客户。除非事先获得客户同意，否则不可将客户的持仓拨入客户按金对销户口内。客户按金对销户口的持仓按毛额基准列帐，但按净额基准计算按金。期货结算所参与者必须确保在客户按金对销户口内列帐用作对销按金的所有持仓，均可与其内部纪录对帐；及
(e) 庄家户口－用作记录及维持期货结算所参与者本身所进行或根据其任何安排进行的庄家活动所产生之交易及持仓。该户口的持仓按净额基准收取持仓的按金。


---

## 第98题 (ID: 244906)

### 中文题目

A公司是期交所的“经纪”类别参与者，专门为其他机构投资者提供交易服务。A公司自身没有计划建立独立的结算后台系统。根据《期货结算所规则》，A公司应如何安排其通过期交所订立的期货合约的结算事宜？
A. A公司必须自己向期货结算所注册成为“结算参与者”，否则其交易无法结算。
B. A公司可以继续交易，其交易将自动由期货结算所以“非结算所参与者”的身份代为结算。
C. A公司须获得一名“全面结算参与者”代表其记录、登记及结算其订立的每一份合约。
D. A公司因其“经纪”身份，其所有交易将自动由期交所负责结算，无需另行安排。


### English

Company A is a “Broker” category participant of the Futures Exchange, specializing in providing trading services for other institutional investors. Company A itself has no plans to establish an independent back-office clearing system. Under the Clearing House Rules, how should Company A arrange for the clearing of futures contracts it executes on the Futures Exchange?
A. Company A must register itself with the Clearing House as a “Clearing Participant”; otherwise,its trades cannot be cleared.
B. Company A may continue trading; its trades will be automatically cleared by the Clearing House under the status of a “Non-Clearing Participant”.
C. Company A must engage a “General Clearing Participant” to record,register,and clear each contract it executes on its behalf.
D. Due to its “Broker” status,all its trades will be automatically cleared by the Futures Exchange; no separate arrangement is needed.


**正确答案：C**


### 答案解析

A错误。A公司可以选择不成为结算所参与者，并非必须注册为“结算参与者”。
B错误。非结算所参与者并无进行结算的权利，期货结算所不会自动为其结算。
C正确。根据规则，非结算所参与者并无进行结算的权利，惟须按照《期货结算所规则》获得一名全面结算参与者代表其记录、登记及结算其订立的每一份合约。
D错误。期交所负责交易，不负责结算。结算由期货结算所及其参与者负责。


### Explanation

A is incorrect. Company A may choose not to become a Clearing Participant; it is not mandatory to register as a “Clearing Participant”.
B is incorrect. Non-Clearing Participants do not have the right to clear trades. The Clearing House will not clear trades for them automatically.
C is correct. According to the rules, Non-Clearing Participants do not have the right to clear trades, but they must, in accordance with the Clearing House Rules, obtain a General Clearing Participant to record, register, and clear each contract they execute on their behalf.
D is incorrect. The Futures Exchange is responsible for trading, not clearing. Clearing is the responsibility of the Clearing House and its participants.


### 温习册出处

期货结算所参与者类别
期交所参与者不一定会成为期货结算所参与者。不具期货结算所参与者资格的期交所参与者被称为非结算所参与者。
期交所参与者可向期货结算所注册成为以下两个类别的结算所参与者：
(a) 全面结算参与者；或
(b) 结算参与者。
根据《期货结算所规则》，非结算所参与者并无进行结算的权利，惟须按照《期货结算所规则》获得一名全面结算参与者代表其记录、登记及结算其订立的每一份合约。


---

## 第99题 (ID: 244907)

### 中文题目

一家已在香港注册的证券公司，计划扩展业务至期货市场。该公司已成功注册成为期交所参与者，并以其注册名称“ABC证券有限公司”运营。现在，该公司希望进一步申请成为香港期货结算有限公司的参与者。根据期货结算所参与者的基本申请条件，以下哪项是该公司必须满足的前提？
A. 该公司必须首先将其运营名称从“ABC证券有限公司”更改为一个包含“期货结算”字样的新名称。
B. 该公司必须以书面形式承诺同意接受《期货结算所规则》的约束。
C. 该公司必须证明其主要业务地点位于香港岛，而非九龙或新界。
D. 该公司必须获得至少五家现有期货结算所参与者的联合推荐信。


### English

A securities company already registered in Hong Kong plans to expand its business into the futures market. The company has successfully registered as a Futures Exchange participant and operates under its registered name “ABC Securities Limited”. Now, the company wishes to further apply to become a participant of HKFE Clearing Corporation Limited. According to the basic application conditions for a Clearing Participant, which of the following is a prerequisite that the company must fulfill?
A. The company must first change its operating name from “ABC Securities Limited” to a new name containing the words “Futures Clearing”.
B. The company must provide a written undertaking agreeing to be bound by the Clearing House Rules.
C. The company must demonstrate that its principal place of business is located on Hong Kong Island,not in Kowloon or the New Territories.
D. The company must obtain joint reference letters from at least five existing Clearing Participants.


**正确答案：B**


### 答案解析

A错误。申请人应以其为期交所参与者的注册名称营运（特定例外除外），无需更名。
B正确。申请人必须以书面承诺同意接受《期货结算所规则》约束，这是明确列出的条件之一。
C错误。申请条件中未对业务地点在香港的具体区域作出要求。
D错误。申请条件中未要求提供现有参与者的推荐信。


### Explanation

A is incorrect. The applicant should operate under its registered name as a Futures Exchange participant (with specific exceptions), and a name change is not required.
B is correct. The applicant must provide a written undertaking agreeing to be bound by the Clearing House Rules. This is one of the explicitly listed conditions.
C is incorrect. The application conditions do not specify requirements regarding the specific district within Hong Kong for the place of business.
D is incorrect. The application conditions do not require reference letters from existing participants.


### 温习册出处

成为期货结算所参与者的条件
期货结算所参与者资格的申请人必须：
(a) 注册为期交所参与者，并以其为期交所参与者的注册名称营运（身份为注册机构的全面结算参与者除外，其应根据《证券及期货条例》注册的同一名称注册）；
(b) 符合财政资源规定；
(c) 以书面承诺同意接受《期货结算所规则》约束；
(d) 已悉数支付期货结算所要求的按金；及
(e) 遵从批准通知内指明的任何其他条件。


---

## 第100题 (ID: 244908)

### 中文题目

张先生是某期货交易商的HKATS系统操作员。他收到一位客户的买入某期货合约的指令。根据期交所的交易流程规定，张先生接下来应如何操作？
A. 张先生应先将该指令记录在案，待市场行情达到客户指定价格时，再手动通过电话向交易大厅报单。
B. 张先生应随即通过HKATS电子交易系统终端机在系统上输入该客户的买卖盘指令。
C. 张先生需要将客户指令转交给另一位拥有不同权限的交易员，由该交易员决定是否及何时输入系统。
D. 张先生必须等待其公司内部风险管理部门的预批准后，才能将指令输入任何交易系统。


### English

Mr. Zhang is a HKATS system operator for a futures dealer. He receives an order from a client to buy a certain futures contract. According to the Futures Exchange&#039;s trading process requirements, what should Mr. Zhang do next?
A. Mr. Zhang should first record the order and then manually phone the order to the trading floor when the market reaches the client&#039;s specified price.
B. Mr. Zhang should immediately input the client&#039;s order into the system via a HKATS electronic trading system terminal.
C. Mr. Zhang needs to forward the client order to another trader with different permissions,who will decide whether and when to input it into the system.
D. Mr. Zhang must wait for pre-approval from his company&#039;s internal risk management department before inputting the order into any trading system.


**正确答案：B**


### 答案解析

A错误。所有交易相关事务应采用HKATS等电子交易系统进行，不应采用电话报单等非指定方式。
B正确。当客户向期交所参与者作出指示时，其HKATS系统操作员可随即透过HKATS终端机在系统上输入客户的指示。
C错误。操作员在收到客户指示后应随即输入，无需转交他人决定。
D错误。虽然公司内部可能有风控流程，但规则层面描述的操作流程是操作员随即输入指令。


### Explanation

A is incorrect. All matters related to orders and contract execution should be conducted using the HKATS electronic trading system or other designated systems, not non-designated methods such as phoning orders to the floor.
B is correct. When a client gives an instruction to a Futures Exchange participant, its HKATS system operator may immediately input the client&#039;s instruction into the system via a HKATS terminal.
C is incorrect. The operator should input the instruction immediately upon receipt; there is no need to forward it for a decision by another person.
D is incorrect. Although companies may have internal risk control procedures, the operational process described at the rules level is for the operator to input the instruction immediately.


### 温习册出处

透过 HKATS 电子交易系统进行交易
所有与买盘、沽盘及期交所合约订定相关的事务应采用 HKATS 电子交易系统或期交所董事会指定的有关其他交易系统进行。各期交所参与者须经批准并于期交所注册后，方可透过 HKATS 电子交易系统进行交易。HKATS 电子交易系统可透过输入期交所分配的 HKATS 电子交易系统用户名称及密码进入。此外，各期交所参与者须获期交所批准，以买卖各特定类别的期货合约产品。
倘某客户向期交所参与者作出指示，则其 HKATS 电子交易系统操作员可随即透过 HKATS 电子交易系统终端机在系统上输入客户的指示。接着，HKATS 电子交易系统将根据价格／时间优先权方式将相关买卖盘自动对盘。作为经纪的期交所参与者，将即时确认为客户执行指示，同时有关交易会被传送至期货结算所进行登记及结算。香港期货结算有限公司（“期货结算所”）的参与者资格
期货结算所负责为于期交所完成的交易进行结算。每一个期货结算所参与者必须为期交所参与者。任何非期交所参与者的申请将不被接纳。


---

## 第101题 (ID: 244909)

### 中文题目

一家资产管理公司计划成为期交所参与者，以便直接为其管理的客户基金以及公司自营盘交易期货合约。根据期交所参与者的业务活动类别划分，该公司应当申请成为以下哪一类别的参与者？
A. 交易员
B. 经纪
C. 期货交易商
D. 商户交易商


### English

An asset management company plans to become a Futures Exchange participant to trade futures contracts directly for both the client funds it manages and its own proprietary book. According to the classification of business activity categories for Futures Exchange participants, which category should the company apply for?
A. Trader
B. Broker
C. Futures Dealer
D. Merchant Trader


**正确答案：C**


### 答案解析

A错误。交易员类别仅有权以其本身帐户进行交易，不能为客户账户交易。
B错误。经纪类别仅有权为其本身账户或其他期交所参与者的账户进行交易，不能为“任何其他人士”（即非参与者的客户）的账户交易。
C正确。期货交易商有权为本身帐户、其他期交所参与者的帐户及任何其他人士的帐户进行合约交易，符合该公司为自营盘和客户基金交易的需求。
D错误。商户交易商仅能为其本身账户交易，且其期货业务必须从属于其主要业务，这与专业资产管理公司的性质不符。


### Explanation

A is incorrect. The Trader category is only entitled to trade for its own account and cannot trade for client accounts.
B is incorrect. The Broker category is only entitled to trade for its own account or act as an agent for other Futures Exchange participants. It cannot trade for the accounts of "any other persons" (i.e., clients who are not participants).
C is correct. The Futures Dealer category is entitled to trade contracts for its own account, for the accounts of other Futures Exchange participants, and for the accounts of any other persons. This meets the company&#039;s needs to trade for both its proprietary book and client funds.
D is incorrect. The Merchant Trader category can only trade for its own account, and its futures business must be ancillary to its principal business, which does not align with the nature of a professional asset management company.


### 温习册出处

期交所参与者类别
虽然证监会就从事期货合约交易及就此提供意见的公司所发出的牌照，并无特定指明其可进行的业务活动类别，但期交所参与者可进行并获期交所发出认可的业务活动类别，共有 4 个。有关类别已载列于《期交所规则》，各类别均拥有《期交所规则》所载的权利及责任。
该 4 个类别为：
(a) 交易员－仅有权以其本身帐户进行合约交易；
(b) 经纪－仅有权以其本身帐户进行合约交易，或担任期交所参与者（而非其他人士）的代理人；
(c) 期货交易商－有权为本身帐户、其他期交所参与者的帐户及任何其他人士的帐户进行合约交易；及
(d) 商户交易商－仅有权为其本身帐户进行合约交易，而该等期货业务必须从属于该商户交易商或其控股公司的主要业务。
要成为以上其中一个类别的期交所参与者，申请人必须符合上述适用条件。就申请期交所参与者资格交易员类别的公司而言，其股份及债务资本以及其管理及控制必须全属一名个人拥有。


---

## 第102题 (ID: 244910)

### 中文题目

一家在香港注册成立的有限公司计划申请成为香港期货交易所有限公司的交易参与者。该公司已具备从事第2类受规管活动的证监会牌照，并符合相关的财政资源要求。在准备申请材料时，该公司管理层需要确认以下哪项是期交所规定的必备申请条件？
A. 公司必须证明其主要业务活动位于中国大陆，以促进两地市场互联互通。
B. 公司必须授权一名董事代表公司签署受《期交所规则》约束的承诺书，并提供相关董事会决议的核证副本。
C. 公司必须已在期交所拥有至少一年的模拟交易记录，以证明其交易能力。
D. 公司必须承诺将其大部分客户资产托管于期交所指定的某一结算银行。


### English

A limited company incorporated in Hong Kong plans to apply to become a trading participant of Hong Kong Futures Exchange Limited. The company already holds an SFC license for Type 2 regulated activity and meets the relevant financial resources requirements. While preparing the application materials, the company&#039;s management needs to confirm which of the following is a mandatory application requirement stipulated by the Futures Exchange?
A. The company must demonstrate that its principal business activities are located in Mainland China to promote market connectivity.
B. The company must authorize a director to sign the undertaking to be bound by the Futures Exchange Rules on its behalf and provide a certified copy of the relevant board resolution.
C. The company must have at least one year of simulated trading records on the Futures Exchange to prove its trading capability.
D. The company must commit to depositing the majority of its client assets with a specific settlement bank designated by the Futures Exchange.


**正确答案：B**


### 答案解析

A错误。成为期交所参与者的条件中未要求公司主要业务活动位于中国大陆。
B正确。申请人须按格式填妥申请书，包括受《期交所规则》约束的承诺书，连同授权一名董事代表公司签署承诺书的董事会会议纪录核证副本。
C错误。成为期交所参与者的条件中未要求提供模拟交易记录。
D错误。成为期交所参与者的条件中未要求对客户资产托管于特定银行作出承诺。


### Explanation

A is incorrect. The conditions for becoming a Futures Exchange participant do not require the company&#039;s principal business activities to be located in Mainland China.
B is correct. The applicant must complete the application form in the prescribed manner and submit it to the Futures Exchange, including an undertaking to be bound by the Futures Exchange Rules, together with a certified copy of the board meeting minutes authorizing a director to sign the undertaking on the company&#039;s behalf.
C is incorrect. The conditions for becoming a Futures Exchange participant do not require providing simulated trading records.
D is incorrect. The conditions for becoming a Futures Exchange participant do not require a commitment to deposit client assets with a specific bank.


### 温习册出处

成为期交所参与者的条件
具备期交所参与者资格的申请人，一般须为于香港注册成立的有限公司，并须作出下列事项：
(a) 按规定的格式填妥申请书并提交予期交所，包括受《期交所规则》约束的承诺书，连同授权一名董事代表公司签署承诺书的董事会会议纪录核证副本；
(b) 符合《证券及期货（财政资源）规则》（“《财政资源规则》”）及期交所其他财政规定；
(c) 向期交所悉数支付一切所需费用；
(d) 证明无理由支持其不获证监会发牌或注册以从事第 2 类受规管活动；
(e) 持有期交所交易权；及
(f) 遵守批准通知书内规定的任何其他条件。


---
